SMIS 2 RE, KUN RIG RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD SENG KHRI BCAS SMIS 2

RE, NGAN SONG SBYONG BA'I RGYAL BO SOGS BZHI LA KHRI BCAS SMIS 1.50

RE, DE NAS SPYAN MA NAS 'BEB PA'I BAR GYI LHA SO GNYIS PO LA PAD

'DAB BCAS MTHO TSAD SMIS 1 RE, RTZEG BAR MA LA 'OD DPAG

@711 MED RMA BYAS BTEGS PA'I KHRI BCAS SMIS 2 RE, G-YAS SU SPYAN RAS

GZIGS DANG G-YON DU PHYAG NA RDO RJE GNYIS SMIS 1 RE, DE'I MTHA'

SKOR LA 'OD DPAG MED STONG SKU LDUG DGOS, RTZEG STENG MA STE BUM

PA'I NANG LA RJE TZONG KHA BA SENG KHRI BCAS SMIS 2.333 RE, RGYAL TSAB

RJE DANG MKHAS GRUB RJE GNYIS LA SENG KHRI BCAS SMIS 1.60 RE, RJE

TSA KHO BA MKHAN CHEN NGAG DBANG GRAGS PA, 'DUL 'DZIN GRAGS

PA RGYAL MTSAN, 'KHOR DAG PA RNAM BRGYAD RNAMS LA MTHO TSAD

SMIS 1.20 TZAM YOD SNYAM STE DA LTA BZHENG BZHIN LAGS, BYAMS

PA LA GZUNGS 'JUG PHUL ZIN PAS, GZUNGS 'JUG RGYAS PA TSAR

NYER GCIG DMIGS BRTZE MA DANG, GZUNGS CHEN SDE LNGA, AA

RA PA TZA, YIG BRGYA RNAMS SHIN TU MANG NGO, ,SENG KHRI'I NANG

TSOGS BDAG DANG 'DZAM DKAR GTER SGRUB DANG, MKHAS GRUB

RJE DANG PAn CHEN BLO BZANG CHOS RGYAN LUGS KYI GNOD SBYIN PHO

'KHOR MO 'KHOR RGYAS PA, RJE SKU MANG BO DANG, 'JIGS BYED KYI

SKU SOGS BRIS 'BUR MANG BO DANG BLA BRANG BKRA SHIS 'KHYIL NAS

GNANG BA'I KUN MKHYEN RIN PO CHE'I 'DRA SKU THUGS KAR GZHUG

KHONG GI GDUNG TSA LAS BZHENGS PA'I RJE SKU DANG, MI 'KHRUGS PA,

TSE LHA RNAM GSUM DANG, TSA TSA SOGS GZHUNG NAS JI LTAR GSUNGS

PA LTAR DBU DANG SKU'I STOD SMAD BAR GSUM DU PHUL, YUM RGYAS PA

@712 'BUM TSAR GSUM DANG, BRGYAD STONG BA SOGS BZANG DRUG DANG DRI

BZANG SOGS KYIS BYUR BUR GTAMS SO, ,RTZEG 'OG MAR BYAMS

PA GTZO 'KHOR GSUM, KUN RIG RTZA LHA SO BDUN TE LHA BZHI BCU,

RTZEG BAR MA LA 'OD DPAG MED GTZO 'KHOR GSUM, BUM PAR RJE

YAB SRAS GSUM DANG, TSA KHO NGAG DBANG GRAGS PA, 'DUL

'DZIN, 'KHOR DAG PA RNAM BRGYAD DE BCU GSUM BCAS KHYON SKU

'DRA NGA DRUG PO LHA SHING SHUG PAS BZOS DANG BZO BZHIN PA LAGS

SHING, SNA TSOGS BZO BO'AM BI SHVA KARMA DANG MI GNYIS PA RGYA NAG

PO'I YUL LAS KRE CANG GI SOR MO'I 'PHRUL LDAN RNAM PA'I SGYU 'PHRUL

LAS BYUNG BA'O, ,DE LTAR RDO BZO SHING BZO GSER ZANGS BZO BA LHA

BZO RNAMS KYI LAS GLA LA SOGS RAGS RTZIS SGOR KHRI TSO SO BZHI SONG

ZIN TO, ,SGOR MO'I 'DANG SONG NA STENG 'OG BAR GSUM LA

GSER TSON BYUG RGYU DANG, GYANG RA PHYI'I MTHA' SKOR LA 'KHOR KHANG

BZHENG RGYU SOGS THUGS BKOD GNANG YOD,

LEGS BYAS TSOGS GNYIS GANGS KYI RI LAS 'ONGS PA'I RNAM

PAR THAR BA MA DROS KLUNG CHEN LAS, ,THA MA'I CHA PHRAN CHU THIGS

TZAM ZHIG BKOD PA DAD PA'I CHU GTER 'PHEL BA'I ZLA 'OD 'DI, ,

BSKRUN PA'I DGE BAS BDAG SOGS MAR GYUR SEMS CAN THAMS

CAD THAR BA'I KHANG BZANG BGROD PA'I PHYIR, ,THEM SKAS DANG BO

@713 THEG PA MCHOG GI DGE BA'I BSHES KYIS DGYES BZHIN RJES SU 'DZIN

GYUR CIG ,CES PA 'DI NI LAS KYI SNE MO BA RNAMS KYIS KHA SKONG ZHIG DGOS

ZHES YANG YANG BSKUL BA LTAR, PHRAN LA'ANG GANG THAD NAS 'OS MED KYANG

YANG TSA BSLAB GSUM RGYA MTSO'I ZIN BRIS LA 'PHRI SNON CUNG ZAD BYAS TE RAB

GNAS SHING KHYI LO'I HOR ZLA DGU BA'I DMAR PHYOGS RGYAL BA GNYIS PA'I (SPYI
